URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS396796354	2020-06-18 09:51:47	32701	species	Nashville Warbler	Leiothlypis ruficapilla			1				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	Clark	US-NV-003		33			Las Vegas--Floyd Lamb Park at Tule Springs	L139900	H	36.3249025	-115.2665940	2016-04-30	11:30:00	obsr221195	S29312907	Traveling	P22	EBIRD	150	2.414		2	1		0	1	0		The weather was very atypical, with rain at my place from roughly 4 AM to 10 AM, and I assume the pattern was similar at the park, along with wind on the western edges or exposed areas and 55 degree weather when we started.  There were very few people at the park except the many campers affiliated with some group.  I am not sure why but whenever they have one of these group camp events, the weather is usually miserable.  However, it seemed to be quite good for migrants and we saw many species that we would not normally expect.  Although we got there on the late side of the morning, I think it likely that the birds had not been able to feed much with the rain, but were quite voracious feeders once it had stopped for a bit.
